{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_014RsDpK22EoF9ECjduDwdXG","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01TSKHVRcfcYGrocj52KGqP7","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/BUG_REPORT.md","content":"# Bug Report: Ad-Blocker Cache Corruption Crash\n\n## Summary\n\nqutebrowser crashes on startup when the ad-blocker filter cache file is corrupted or contains invalid data. The application raises an unhandled `adblock.DeserializationError` exception, preventing the user from using the browser until they manually delete the cache file.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nIn `/app/qutebrowser/components/braveadblock.py`, the `read_cache()` method (lines 204-230) attempts to handle deserialization errors, but has incomplete exception handling:\n\n### Current Code (Buggy)\n```python\ndef read_cache(self) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Initialize the adblocking engine from cache file.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        cache_exists = self._cache_path.is_file()\n    except OSError:\n        logger.error(\"Failed to read adblock cache\", exc_info=True)\n        return\n\n    if cache_exists:\n        logger.debug(\"Loading cached adblock data: %s\", self._cache_path)\n        try:\n            self._engine.deserialize_from_file(str(self._cache_path))\n        except ValueError as e:\n            if str(e) != \"DeserializationError\":\n                # All Rust exceptions get turned into a ValueError by\n                # python-adblock\n                raise\n            message.error(\"Reading adblock filter data failed (corrupted data?). \"\n                          \"Please run :adblock-update.\")\n        else:\n            if (...):\n                message.info(\"Run :adblock-update to get adblock lists.\")\n```\n\n### The Problem\n\nThe code only catches `ValueError`, but when the cache file is corrupted, the `adblock.Engine.deserialize_from_file()` method raises `adblock.DeserializationError`, which is **NOT** a subclass of `ValueError`. Therefore:\n\n1. When the cache is corrupted, `adblock.DeserializationError` is raised\n2. The `except ValueError` clause does not match\n3. The exception propagates uncaught\n4. The application crashes before the user can even see the browser window\n\n### Exception Hierarchy\n\n- `adblock.DeserializationError` extends `adblock.BlockerException` (not `ValueError`)\n- The current code assumes all deserialization errors will be `ValueError` instances\n- This assumption is incorrect based on the actual behavior of the `adblock` library\n\n## Expected Behavior\n\nThe application should:\n1. Catch the deserialization error gracefully\n2. Log an appropriate error message\n3. Continue running without ad-blocking (as intended by the message.error() call)\n4. Allow the user to browse and run `:adblock-update` to rebuild the cache\n\n## How to Reproduce\n\n1. Create a corrupted cache file at `~/.local/share/qutebrowser/adblock-cache.dat`\n2. Populate it with invalid data (e.g., random bytes)\n3. Start qutebrowser\n4. The application will crash with `adblock.DeserializationError: DeserializationError`\n\n## Regression Test\n\nA comprehensive regression test has been provided at `/workspace/regression_test.py` that demonstrates this bug by:\n\n1. Creating a temporary data directory\n2. Creating a BraveAdBlocker instance\n3. Writing corrupted data to the cache file\n4. Calling `read_cache()`\n5. Verifying that the unhandled exception is raised (on buggy code) or handled gracefully (on fixed code)\n\n### Running the Test\n\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null --timeout=60 /workspace/regression_test.py\n```\n\nOn the buggy code, both tests will FAIL with the message:\n```\nFailed: Corrupted cache should be handled gracefully, but got unhandled DeserializationError: DeserializationError\n```\n\nThis indicates the bug is present. When the bug is fixed, the tests will PASS because the exception will be caught and handled properly.\n\n## Fix Strategy\n\nThe exception handling should be updated to:\n1. Catch both `ValueError` and `adblock.DeserializationError` (and potentially other adblock exceptions)\n2. Or catch a broader exception type like `Exception` to ensure all deserialization errors are handled\n3. Or check the exception type instead of the message\n\nThe most robust fix would be:\n```python\ntry:\n    self._engine.deserialize_from_file(str(self._cache_path))\nexcept Exception as e:\n    # Catch all deserialization errors from the adblock library\n    message.error(\"Reading adblock filter data failed (corrupted data?). \"\n                  \"Please run :adblock-update.\")\n```\n\nThis ensures any error from the adblock library during deserialization is handled gracefully.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1132,"cache_read_input_tokens":71591,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1132},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7045ecb1-084c-42d8-a6c8-44b4172b152a","uuid":"bf9ece82-0180-43ad-8319-de2ae1ed967c"}
